  * grade_story_103.txt (grade=7.8)
    While generally original, the story occasionally slips into somewhat predictable emotional territory with phrases like "joyful agony" and "terrible beauty" that feel slightly formulaic. The ghostly daughter's forgiveness is beautifully executed but treads familiar ground in redemption narratives. However, the integration of the magical mirror with concrete personal objects creates a fresh approach to exploring guilt and forgiveness. The narrative voice maintains consistency throughout, with emotional nuance generally shown rather than told.

  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=6.8)

The spiritual transformation follows somewhat predictable patterns of revelation. The ending, while thematically appropriate, relies on abstract statements about wholeness rather than concrete, specific imagery that would make the transformation more visceral and unique.

The prose occasionally veers toward the ornate but generally maintains emotional authenticity and logical consistency throughout.
